\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02390}02390     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02391}02391     \textcolor{comment}{// The various boundary/region lookups now need updating to account for the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02392}02392     \textcolor{comment}{// newly added/removed elements. This will be done in two stages:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02393}02393     \textcolor{comment}{// Step 1: Add the new elements to the vector of elements in the same region}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02394}02394     \textcolor{comment}{//         as the original corner element, and then delete the originals.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02395}02395     \textcolor{comment}{//         Updating this lookup makes things easier in the following step.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02396}02396     \textcolor{comment}{// Step 2: Regenerate the two more specific lookups: One which gives the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02397}02397     \textcolor{comment}{//         elements on a given boundary in a given region, and the other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02398}02398     \textcolor{comment}{//         which maps elements on a given boundary in a given region to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02399}02399     \textcolor{comment}{//         element's face index on that boundary.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02400}02400     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02401}02401     \textcolor{comment}{// N.B. the lookup Triangular\_facet\_vertex\_boundary\_coordinate is setup in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02402}02402     \textcolor{comment}{// the call to setup\_boundary\_element\_info() above so doesn't need}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{tet__mesh_8h_source_l02403}02403     \textcolor{comment}{// additional work.}}
